article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">BEIJING, March 19 (Reuters) - China will likely develop national standards for ‌post-quantum cryptography in the next three years as it pours funds into in 2024 and is aiming to achieve full industry migration by 2035. China last year, however, issued a global call to solicit new standards.</div><div data-testid="element" class="article-body-module__element__5eCce"></div><div data-testid="paragraph-4" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">Finance and energy would ​be the priority sectors for migration to post-quantum cryptography given the sensitivity of the ​data, said Wang Xiaoyun, professor at Tsinghua University&#x27;s Institute for Advanced Study.</div><div data-testid="paragraph-5" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">&quot;I personally think that the next ‌three-to-five-year ⁠period is potentially one of explosive growth for post-quantum cryptography industry migration (in China),&quot; she said on the sidelines of the National People&#x27;s Congress parliamentary meetings in Beijing that <a data-testid="Link" referrerPolicy="no-referrer-when-downgrade" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/chinas-parliament-rolls-out-economic-political-blue-print-heres-what-you-need-2026-03-05/" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__inherit-color__PhuPF text-module__inherit-font__1P1hv text-module__inherit-size__EyiQW link-module__link__INqxZ link-module__underline_default__-okuC">concluded</a> last week.</div><div data-testid="element" class="article-body-module__element__5eCce"></div><div data-testid="paragraph-6" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">Unlike most international researchers in the U.S. and elsewhere, Chinese post-quantum cryptographers have focused on ​developing &quot;structureless lattice&quot; algorithms like ​S-Cloud+.</div><div data-testid="paragraph-7" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">International standards based ⁠on algebraic lattices &quot;have some degree of security degradation,&quot; Wang said. &quot;But structureless cryptographic algorithms basically do not have this problem.&quot;</div><div data-testid="paragraph-8" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">In a first, China ​made a homegrown operating system for quantum computers that is open ​source available ⁠for online download last month, state media reported.</div><div data-testid="element" class="article-body-module__element__5eCce"></div><div data-testid="paragraph-9" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">Google and other tech industry leaders have urged governments to accelerate adoption of post-quantum cryptography. The Trump administration&#x27;s cyber strategy, released last week, pledges ⁠to sustain ​U.S. dominance in post-quantum cryptography and artificial intelligence.</div><div data-testid="paragraph-10" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">South ​Korea plans to implement post-quantum cryptography across a broad range of industries by 2035, with a pilot 2025-2028 transition ​plan targeting critical sectors like energy and healthcare.</div><div data-testid="element" class="article-body-module__element__5eCce"></div><div data-testid="paragraph-11" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__small_body__gOmDf article-body-module__paragraph__Ts-yF">(This story has been refiled to correct the spelling of &#x27;cryptography&#x27; in the headline)</div><div class="article-body-module__element__5eCce"><p data-testid="SignOff" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__extra_small__8Buss body-module__full_width__kCIGb body-module__extra_small_body__Bfz20 sign-off-module__text__LQAMP">Reporting by Laurie Chen; Editing by Edwina Gibbs</p></div><p data-testid="Body" dir="ltr" class="text-module__text__0GDob text-module__dark-grey__UFC18 text-module__regular__qJJtA text-module__small__sph8i
